[usu. circumstances] 1 xaalad wax la xiriirta; daruuf. e.g. They want to escape the prison but circumstances didn't permit. 2 xaqiiq ama dhacdo, siiba mid aan la sugayn. e.g. His two sons were killed together by circumstance. 3 xaaladda dhaqaale ee qof ku noolyahay. e.g. Some people in Somalia are still in comfortable circumstances.

-under no circumstances, marnaba; si kasta oo xaalad noqoto. e.g. Under no circumstances should you hide the truth.

-under (or in) the circumstances, xaalad darteed, siiba mid xun. e.g. The country was in war, and under the circumstances there was no safe place to hide but to cross the border. -circumstanced adj.

circumstantial (,sarkam'istaanjal) adj. 1 lagu saleeyay wax aan caddayn ama aan la hubin. e.g. The blood found on his clothe is circumstantial evidence. 2 aan ahayn muhiim. 3 bixiya faahfaahin. e.g. The police wrote a circumstantial report of the accident. -circumstantial ity (,sarkam,istaanjii'aaladhi) n.; -circumstantially adv.

conglomerate (kan'galaamarat) v. ku-aruurid; ku-xoomid. e.g. The students conglomerated the teacher. -adj. ku soo aruura ama shamuuma.

conglomeration (kan,galaama'reyshan) n. isku-daryo wax yaalo kala duwan. e.g. The soup was conglomeration of meat, beans, and vegetables.

Congo (‘kaanggaw) n. 1 wabi mara bartamaha Afrika oo ku biya-shuba Badwaynta Atlantic. 2 [often the Congo] ama Republic of the Congo, waddan ku yaal galbeedka Afrika; darisna la ah Central African Republic, Demo cratic Republic of the Congo, Angola, Badwaynta At lantic, Gabon, iyo Cameroon; caasimad, Brazzaville; luuqad, French.

 Congo

Congo, Democratic Republic of the waddan ku yaal bartamaha Afrika ee xeebaha Badwaynta Atlantic; darisna la ah Sudan, Uganda, Zambia, Angola, Badwaynta Atlantic, Congo, iyo Central African Repub lic; caasimad, Kinshasa; luuqad, French, Kongo, Lingal, Swahili, iyo kuwo kale. Loona aqoonjiray (ilaa 1997) Zaire.

n.; -congratulatory adj.

congratulation (kan,garaaja'leyshan) n. 1 hambalyo {tahnyah}. 2 congratulations, erayo hambalyo iyo tahniyado ah. e.g. Congratulations on your marriage.

congregate (kaang'garageyt) v. ku-soo-ururid; shamuumid; isku-imaatin. e.g. The farmers congregated around the fire.

congregation (,kaanggra'geyshan) n. 1 kulan; isku imaansho {jamaaca}. e.g. Large congregation of birds may harm crops. 2 kulan wayne, siiba mid diin ama arrimo kale la iskugu yimaado {maxfal}.

congregational (,kaanggra'geyshanal) adj. la xiriira kulan ama shir wayne.

congress (‘kaanggaras) n. 1 gole baarlamaan ee waddan {majmac}. 2 shir ama shirar isdaba joog ah oo ay iskugu yimaadaan kooxo xiisaynaya arin gaar ah. e.g. An inter national congress of physicians. 3 urur siyaasadeed. 4 wada-galmoodyo nin iyo naag. -congressional adj.

congruent (kan'guruwanti) adj. 1 Xisaab xaglo ama qaabab is le'eg. e.g. Congruent triangles. 2 israaci kara; la isku dari karo. -congruence n.; -congruency n.

congruous (‘kaanggarawas) adj. la mid congruent. e.g. This example is congruous with yours. -congruity {munaasabah}n.; -congruously adv.

conical (‘kaanikal) adj. qaab toobin leh. e.g. Naasa-hablood Mountains are conical. -conically adv.

conifer (‘kaanafar) n. geed dhala caleemo af-fiiqan iyo sal buuran leh, sida geed cananaaska.

coniferous (ka'nifaras) adj. leh caleemo af-dhuuban. e.g. A coniferous tree. -coniferously adv.

conjectural (kan'jekjaral) adj. mala ah ama ku salaysan. e.g. Her statement was entirely conjectural. -conjectur ally adv.

conjecture (kan'jekjar) n. malo ama malayn; odoros; soo jeedin aan lagu salayn wax la hubo. e.g. The conjec tures about Carraweelo's life were many. Is that for sure or is it only conjecture?

-v. -tured, -turing. qiyaasid; odorosid. e.g. The weather man has to conjecture about next week's weather con ditions. Somali politicians conjectured that it would be a bloody civil war. -conjecturable adj.

conjoin (kanjoyn) v. midoobid; isku-darmid. e.g. A theory that conjoins culture and tradition. The two rival war lords eventually conjoined.

conjoint (kan'joynti) adj. mideeya; urursha. e.g. Conjoint family fitness center. -conjointly adv.

conjugal (‘kaanjigal; kan'juugal) adj. guur isku keenay; xiriirka ka dhexeeya nin iyo afadiis. e.g. Conjugal love. -conjugality n.; -conjugally adv.

conjugate (‘kaanja,geyt) v. 1 qaybaha kala duwan ee ficil ka ayada oo loo eegayo qofka, tirada, goorta, iwm. e.g. The present tense of “to be” is conjugates: “I am, you are, he is.” 2 mataanoobid; isku-darmid; isku-xirmid, siiba dhinac guur ama jacayl. 3 Chemistry isku-xirid curiyayaal.

-adj. (kaanjigat) isku xirma; mataanooba.

-n. (kaanjigat) isku-daranyo. -conjugacy (‘kaanjagasi) n.; -conjugative (‘kaanja,geydhiv) adj.

conjugated (‘kaanja,geydhidh) adj. isku-dhaggan; isku qabsan. e.g. The conjugated rooms shared a dinning area. Eray kale oo la mid ah conjugate.

conjugation (,kaanja'geyshan) n. 1 Naxwe qaababka kala duwan ee qaybaha ficil ka. 2 isku darmasho. -conjuga tional adj.

conjunct (kan'janagti) adj. isku darma.

conjunction (kan'jangkshan) n. 1 ku darsanyo. e.g. Civil war, in conjunction with famine, made life difficult. 2 xiriiriye; isku xira erayo, weerooyin, ama hadal. e.g. and, but, or, though, and if are conjunctions. = iyo, laakiin, ama, in kasta oo, iyo haddii waa xiriiriyayaal.

-in conjunction, wada-jir. e.g. Medicine was used in conjunction with exercise. -conjunctional adj.; -conjunctionally adv.

conjuncture (kan'jangjar) n. xaalado xun oo isgudagala; arrimo israaca ama isku darma. e.g. The general was faced with a conjuncture in which he must either to sur render or fight.

conjuration (,kaanjuur'eyshan) n. 1 oraaho lagu dhawaaqo ama loogu yeer-yeero sixir. 2 sixir adeegsasho. e.g. He was changed into a donkey by conjuration.

conjure (‘kaanjar) v. 1 samayn sixir ama indhasarcaad. 2 yeerid ama sookicin sixir ama duulal. e.g. She hoped to conjure up the spirit of dead great grandfathers. 3 xasuusad hadal, cod, ur, iwm., ama ka-muuqad maskax. e.g. He hadn't forgotten to conjure up the image of his grandfather. 4 ku-keenid ama ka-dhigid wax la arki karo.

conjure woman (‘kaanjar) n. sixirley; curraafiso; calaqad. conjuror or conjurer (kaanjarar) n. sixiroole; indhasarcaadshe.

Connecticut (ka'nedhakat) gobol ku yaal waqooyi-bariga US, ee xeebaha Badwaynta Atlantic; magaalamadax, Hartford.

connection (ka'nekshan) n. 1 isku xirnaansho. 2 xiriirka labo dhinac ka dhexeeya. e.g. Our connection with their business had lasted over five years. 3 isku xirnaansho fiilyooyin koronto. e.g. I think we have a bad connec tion in the line. 4 xiriir ka dhaxeeyo. e.g. We have no connection with that guy. 5 connections, ku meeryo, siiba gaadiid kale; baddalasho gaadiid. e.g. They arrived late and missed their train connections. 6 xidid; xigaalo. e.g. She is connection of mine by marriage. 7 qof iibiya ama keena maandooriye. e.g. He is on of her Qaad con nections.

-in connection with, xiriir ama lug ku leh. e.g. They were arrested several people in connection with alleged criminal damage. -connectional adj.

connivance (ka'naayvanis) n. ka jeesasho danbi ama ka qaybgalyo.

connive (ka'naayv) v. connive at/in, 1 ka-indhasaabad dabni lagalo; kuma-arag kuma-maqlin. e.g. The guard connived at my escaping. 2 ku-kaalmayn sharci la jabaninyo, siiba qarsoodi. e.g. Corrupted officers of the police connived with bank robbers. [as adj.] conniving, e.g. A ruthless and conniving warlord. -conniver n.

connote (ka'nawt) v. sarbeebid; maldahid, siiba eray, dareen, ama fikrad. -connotative (‘kaana,teydhiv) adj. connubial (ka'nuubiyal) adj. guur ka dhaxeeyo ama xiriir nin iyo xaaski. -connubiality (ka,nuubi'yaalidhi) n.; - connubially adv.

conquest (‘kaan,kuwesti) n. 1 qabsasho; ka guulaysasho; furasho. e.g. The conquest of Africa by Europeans. 2 dabargooyo; hanasho. e.g. The conquest of disease.

consanguineous (,kaan,saang'guwiniyas) adj. ka xiriira dhinac ab iyo isir; qaraabo oday ah. e.g. Many people prefer to have a consanguineous marriages. -consan guinity (-'guwinidhi) n.

conscience (‘kaanjanis) n. damiir; dareen qof kala tusa sax iyo khalad. e.g. She had a guilty conscience about her lie. -conscienceless adj.

conscientious (,kaanji'yenjas) adj. 1 damiir leh; qof sameeya waxa saxda ah, siiba hawl ama xil saaran. e.g. A consci entious clerk arrived on time. 2 lagu sameeyay si taxaddar iyo hufnaan leh. e.g. Conscientious work. - conscientiously adv. -conscientiousness {idraak} n.

conscientious objector n. qof dareenkiisu u diido in uu ka qaybqaato ciidan, dagaalna u arka in uu khaladyahay. - conscientious objection n.

conscious (‘kaanshas) adj. 1 miyir-qab ah; dareen jooga. e.g. He fainted and lost his conscious. 2 ogsoon; ogaalqab ah. e.g. We were conscious of his hostility 3 dareen dhiba qofka. e.g. She was little conscious in her appearance. 4 danayn ama walaacin qof wax gaar ah. 5 kas ah; ulakac ah. e.g. That was a conscious lie. -consciously adv.
